        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer989693084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16818357703119834783"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'Being with Colton is not easy. It's hard. It's work. But if I think about my life before him, and my life with him... the struggle and work is worth all of it.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Genre:</b> YA characters intended for an older audience<br/><b>Cover:</b> 7/10<br/><b>Writing:</b> 9/10<br/><b>Heroine:</b> 9/10<br/><b>Hero:</b> 9/10<br/><b>Humour:</b> 5/10<br/><b>Hotness:</b> 2/10<br/><b>Romance:</b> 9/10<br/><b>Extra book Details:</b> Approx 130 kindle pages. Heroine POV; 1st person. Stand-alone.<br/><br/>Lilly meets Colton when she's about 10 years old; paid to be his 'buddy', when he moves home, though</span>
  <span id="freeText16818357703119834783" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'Being with Colton is not easy. It's hard. It's work. But if I think about my life before him, and my life with him... the struggle and work is worth all of it.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Genre:</b> YA characters intended for an older audience<br /><b>Cover:</b> 7/10<br /><b>Writing:</b> 9/10<br /><b>Heroine:</b> 9/10<br /><b>Hero:</b> 9/10<br /><b>Humour:</b> 5/10<br /><b>Hotness:</b> 2/10<br /><b>Romance:</b> 9/10<br /><b>Extra book Details:</b> Approx 130 kindle pages. Heroine POV; 1st person. Stand-alone.<br /><br />Lilly meets Colton when she's about 10 years old; paid to be his 'buddy', when he moves home, though gone, she never truly forgets about him.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'I constantly felt like there was some sort of unexplainable viod inside me. Something was missing. You know that feeling like you forgot something? I carried that feeling around with me for years. Years. Then, during the summer I turned fifteen. I found what i'd been looking for.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />What ensues is a beautiful sweet romance over a long period of time, about a girl fighting to understand how a boy ticks and following her heart.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'He's not special. He's extraordinary. To me. And I feel like I am too, when i'm with him.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br /><br />First of all, <b>I was really worried how this book would go.</b> Fiction books with a lead character that has any kind of issues like Aspergers can get it soooo wrong. Sometimes it will come off as condescending, preachy or educational. Other times it will make with the clichéd drama and insensitive characters. 'Jumping Puddles' didn't do any of these things.<br /><br />This brings me on to rating. <b>I deducted half a star, my only reason for not loving this book harder because I felt very anxious. A lot.</b> Lilly went through many struggles with Colton, and the author wrote in many sentences that left me feeling like something really bad was going to happen.<br /><br />I really loved how this book was written, a little correction here and there was needed. But <b>I loved how Lily talked to the reader, and she was so real all her emotions felt right and just how I would feel in that situation.</b><br /><br /><b>Colton was incredibly endearing, I love adorable heroes, and he was definitely one of the best.</b> Lilly was mostly self-assured, honest, understanding, incredibly clever and wore her heart on her sleeve. She was also pretty funny. <b>A lot of this book was beautifully funny.</b><br /><br /><b>I wished I had more time with them both. Such a short but lovely little story. Would have liked to have seen more dialogue between the two characters because what I got was very enjoyable. Recommend for everyone</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16818357703119834783" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8022712575215353818">Beautiful, just beautiful. Colton's story really made me think how difficult is for people to accept diversity, but above all this is about how Love can find us all.<br/><br/>This is one of the most romantic stories I've read in while. I love how sweet the romance was and how much the characters cared for each other. The story is quite short, I flew through it in a couple of hours.<br/><br/>There was one thing I didn't like. Colton's mom not telling Lilly what was going on and thinking that Lilly would be okay to u</span>
  <span id="freeText8022712575215353818" style="display:none">Beautiful, just beautiful. Colton's story really made me think how difficult is for people to accept diversity, but above all this is about how Love can find us all.<br /><br />This is one of the most romantic stories I've read in while. I love how sweet the romance was and how much the characters cared for each other. The story is quite short, I flew through it in a couple of hours.<br /><br />There was one thing I didn't like. Colton's mom not telling Lilly what was going on and thinking that Lilly would be okay to unexpectadly throw that rock on her. In front a whole crowd. I got so, so angry and I wish Lilly had insulted her.<br /><br />As a fan of romantic not graphic <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[loss of innocense/cherry popping stories I found Puddle Jumping to deliver in that front. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That scene was so beautiful and romantic. <br /><br />The book is short so there's a lot of internal dialogue and a little bit of tell don't show which is something I always appreciate even if some people think it's boring. I love to know what's going on on the heroine's mind. I like that Lilly was so brave and loyal to Colton.<br /><br />Please please read this one.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer987792605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16992531742331909516"><b>*****10+++++ Extraordinary Stars******</b><br/><br/><i>(BR with Mel & Patty)</i><br/><br/>This remarkable novel has giving me an infinite amount of hope and inspiration. My vision is still a bit blurry from all the tears I've shed while reading this story, but I'll tell you, best tears I've cried this year. I will never, ever forget the beauty and simplicity of Colton and Lilly's story... This precious book is truly a <b>MUST READ!</b><br/><br/>Lilly and Colton met when they were kids, she was apointed as his babysitter which to her at the mo</span>
  <span id="freeText16992531742331909516" style="display:none"><b>*****10+++++ Extraordinary Stars******</b><br><br><i>(BR with Mel &amp; Patty)</i><br><br>This remarkable novel has giving me an infinite amount of hope and inspiration. My vision is still a bit blurry from all the tears I've shed while reading this story, but I'll tell you, best tears I've cried this year. I will never, ever forget the beauty and simplicity of Colton and Lilly's story... This precious book is truly a <b>MUST READ!</b><br><br>Lilly and Colton met when they were kids, she was apointed as his babysitter which to her at the moment didn't make much sense because she was only a year older than him. Her adventurous personality coupled with her clumsiness caused her to have a few accidents while hanging out with Colton and he was always there to save her and then visit her in the hospital, gifting her a beautiful drawing that would instantly make her feel better. After one too many accidents, Colton's mom decided it was best if she didn't babysit anymore. But they never forgot each other and years later on Lilly's first day of her senior year of high school, a few lockers down from hers, was none other than the beautiful boy who had left a big void inside her heart all those years back.<br><br>Lilly knew Colton had Asperger's, she had learned this fact years ago but never really wanted to find out more, to her he was amazing in every way. On the first day of school they re-kindled their friendship instantly and her devotion for him started. She wanted to know more about him, not only about his disorder though but about his heart. This boy with the striking eyes and incredible talent had stolen a piece of her heart and she was now ready to claim his. Very patiently their friendship turned into a relationship, and little by little they learned and shared together all the little and big things about love. It wasn't always easy for Lilly, but when you love someone you take the good and the bad and never quit trying.<br>Short yet powerful, this story delivers a meaningful message about unconditional love and friendship. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/9d66dc9c-be4b-40e3-b14d-7f984e8dfe04_zps99551d7c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405965831i/10478678._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 9d66dc9c-be4b-40e3-b14d-7f984e8dfe04_zps99551d7c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Every word and every character in this book took my breath away, this is the reason why I love reading, to feel inspired and be moved by stories that will teach me something beautiful. I'm sure everyone who reads this book will be blown away. This little gem will be part of my most treasured library, one I hope to share with my daughters when they are older. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/imagejpg1_zps2b86f4e6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405921316i/10471691._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg1_zps2b86f4e6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My <i>Puddle Jumping</i> Playlist:<br><br>*Always in My Head by Coldplay<br>*Ain't No Reason by Brett Dennen<br>*The Show by Lenka<br>*Nothing More by The Alternate Routes<br>*Tee Shirt by Birdy<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/f1ae7845-7d84-43fb-8786-67263018b31a_zps1e9bcb7f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405889450i/10465861._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo f1ae7845-7d84-43fb-8786-67263018b31a_zps1e9bcb7f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4622977995438040875"><b>5 stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1274.photobucket.com/user/RReadoholic/media/Mobile%20Uploads/20140709_174711-kdcollage_zpsb4sywxwt.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/>Colton and Lilly are childhood friends turn lovers. Its not your typical high school romance though, because Colton has Aspergers.<br/><br/>I loved it. From the face paced story, the writing and the main characters to Coltons condition and their struggle. Individually Lilly was <b>awesome n funny</b>, Colton was <b>adorable and blunt,</b> together they were just<b> too freaking cute!!!</b><br/><br/>Overall it was a <b>quick unforgettable novella</b> with amazing characters. How can a book be <b>so sweet but hurt my heart</b> at the same t</span>
  <span id="freeText4622977995438040875" style="display:none"><b>5 stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1274.photobucket.com/user/RReadoholic/media/Mobile%20Uploads/20140709_174711-kdcollage_zpsb4sywxwt.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>Colton and Lilly are childhood friends turn lovers. Its not your typical high school romance though, because Colton has Aspergers.<br><br>I loved it. From the face paced story, the writing and the main characters to Coltons condition and their struggle. Individually Lilly was <b>awesome n funny</b>, Colton was <b>adorable and blunt,</b> together they were just<b> too freaking cute!!!</b><br><br>Overall it was a <b>quick unforgettable novella</b> with amazing characters. How can a book be <b>so sweet but hurt my heart</b> at the same time?? Amazing! I cant fault it!!!<br><br><i>BR with Daisy and Harriet</i></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1572881506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7231873854354910453">This is one of the best books ever. It's an easy, short read that pulls at all your emotions. Lilly falls in love with a guy that other people think is an idiot, but he isn't, he is smart and different and just dreamy. They fall in love slowly and although their love faces a lot of challenges, his mom being one, they get together and all is tied up nicely in just 120 pages. This is a very inspirational book.</span>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1477185149" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18084830809962491293"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451853837i/17613636.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lilly is only a little child when she meets Colton. She's set to babysit him and she's too young to understand why she needs to babysit a child barely a year younger than her. A clumsy moving danger, Lilly loses her chance to remain friends with Colton after a while. She didn't know then that Colton was special, but she find out several years later when they meet again in an art exhibition of his, where she finds out that he has Asperger. <br/><br/>Now at 17 Colton attends her school and is no longer home</span>
  <span id="freeText18084830809962491293" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451853837i/17613636.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lilly is only a little child when she meets Colton. She's set to babysit him and she's too young to understand why she needs to babysit a child barely a year younger than her. A clumsy moving danger, Lilly loses her chance to remain friends with Colton after a while. She didn't know then that Colton was special, but she find out several years later when they meet again in an art exhibition of his, where she finds out that he has Asperger. <br><br>Now at 17 Colton attends her school and is no longer homeschooled. Lilly and Colton immediately connect once again and their friendship only manages to blossom into something more. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451853837ra/17613637.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was a really beautiful and sweet journey. I've had this book for a very long time and i always wanted to read it. I'm glad I finally did. As it seems, I truly love this kind of reads. My most favorite book has also a character with Asperger syndrome, so I was certain that i would love Colton. But I have to admit that Lilly also won me. Her character was really well written showing that it may not always be easy and how sometimes it could be a struggle, but she would fight for it and I couldn't help but love the progress of their relationship. <br><br>Definitely recommended if you haven't read this one yet!! :))</span>

<div id="review_987136715" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/987136715" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/987136715?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/21825607-puddle-jumping">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=novella">novella</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=ya">ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer987136715" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18137784528971354904">*****4.5 Watercolor Stars*****<br/>(BR with Melissa & Dee)<br/><br/>Lilly Evans and Colton Neely met when they were just ten and nine years old, when she was given the job as his baby sitter.<br/>She never understood why she was given the job of baby sitting since they were so close in age.<br/>But these two formed a strong bond.<br/>She was his companion and the one to bring excitement into his life, which often times landed her in the hospital.<br/>Lilly was very accident prone.<br/>So Colton's mom decides to end Lilly's services fo</span>
  <span id="freeText18137784528971354904" style="display:none">*****4.5 Watercolor Stars*****<br>(BR with Melissa &amp; Dee)<br><br>Lilly Evans and Colton Neely met when they were just ten and nine years old, when she was given the job as his baby sitter.<br>She never understood why she was given the job of baby sitting since they were so close in age.<br>But these two formed a strong bond.<br>She was his companion and the one to bring excitement into his life, which often times landed her in the hospital.<br>Lilly was very accident prone.<br>So Colton's mom decides to end Lilly's services for fear that she may end up killing herself.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/e3dbe9247421d2ab1fe9529a2f015a7d_zps4422fa29.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405915379i/10470875._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e3dbe9247421d2ab1fe9529a2f015a7d_zps4422fa29.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Eight years later, Lilly runs into Colton at a county fair, where he is selling his paintings. She has never forgotten him and had always harbored a crush on him.<br>She learns through local gossip, that Colton has asperger's syndrome.<br><br><br>I found myself comparing this to another book I read with a similar story line, and I have to say this one outshines the other!<br>What made this story so amazing was Lilly!<br>I loved this girl!!<br>She never treated Colton as if he was different.<br>She was quite smitten with him and when he enrolls in her high school she immediately seeks him out and they end up rekindling their friendship as if they hadn't been separated for the last eight years.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/5f343a799905f5996179934a4876a46e_zps82068976.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405915379i/10470876._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5f343a799905f5996179934a4876a46e_zps82068976.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Their relationship turns into something more and I just loved how their family and friends were so supportive of them.<br>Colton's mom was such a kick-ass secondary character.<br>I loved how she could see when Lilly was affected by some of the things Colton would do or was unable to communicate to her.<br>She was always there, providing encouragement.<br><br><br>Lilly was definitely the one that had to make a lot of compromises to make their relationship work, but for the most part, she was understanding. There were a couple moments that it all got to be too much for her, and I just wished to be able to jump into the book and give her a huge hug.<br><br><br><b>I don't believe there's such a thing as conventional love. Love is bending. Love is breaking. Love is constantly learning about the other person until you go crazy because it will never be perfect, but there's no fault in trying.</b><br><br><br>This was such a sweet and beautiful story.<br>I felt my heart bursting with joy while reading it.<br>I fell in love with Colton and Lilly!!<br>And by the epilogue I was pretty much in book heaven!</span>
  <a data-text-id="18137784528971354904" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2194279104" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2194279104" />
    <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell"><img alt="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584062476p2/2190064.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2194279104?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell">Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=kindle-freebie-graveyard">kindle-freebie-graveyard</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=ya-ya-land">ya-ya-land</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=kissing-books">kissing-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2194279104" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6252552983088867999"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>You know those 90s makeover movies where the guy feels like he ought to have "first dibs" on the newly beautiful girl because he liked her when she was "ugly"? This book is basically a gender-flipped version of that, except it's between annoying brat of a heroine and a hero who has Asperger's, and she feels super possessive of him because she feels like she's the only person who treated him like he was "normal" before everyone else reali</span>
  <span id="freeText6252552983088867999" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>You know those 90s makeover movies where the guy feels like he ought to have "first dibs" on the newly beautiful girl because he liked her when she was "ugly"? This book is basically a gender-flipped version of that, except it's between annoying brat of a heroine and a hero who has Asperger's, and she feels super possessive of him because she feels like she's the only person who treated him like he was "normal" before everyone else realized that he was just a normal, even cool guy too. You know what the problem with that is, though? You're assuming that you deserve gold stars for just treating people the way they want to be treated. And this 'heroine' right here? She wants <i>all </i>the gold stars.<br><br><br><br>PUDDLE JUMPING has a 4.22 average rating among my friends, so I was expecting to like it. I wasn't expecting to hate it, or have it fill me with disgust - which it did. First problem for me is that the writing style feels really amateurish and is super chatty, with <i>tons </i>of pointless asides from the narrator that add nothing to the plot. I was willing to roll with it in the beginning, because it's written from the POV of the 'heroine' as a child, but the problem continues - and worsens - over the course of the story. It's just bad writing.<br><br><br><br>Second problem, the treatment of the hero with Asperger's. The whole 'romance' is basically the heroine's big crusade to make the hero her big makeover project. Right away, she goes up to this other girl who's also dating a neurodivergent guy and starts asking for tips. She Googles Asperger's and is totally shocked that <i>people with Asperger's are people, too</i>.<i> </i>She gets a big stick up her bum when the hero gets a job and skips out on prom (not somewhere someone with Asperger's might want to go) to work at his new job, which he loves, and gives him a big lecture about <i>how she is just as important as his job</i>, and then gets his mom on his case to make sure he follows up on all their subsequent dates. At the end of the book, the hero gets an amazing opportunity to pursue his dreams abroad, and the heroine <i>storms out of his party without congratulating him</i>, because she had his future planned out for him and this goes against her plans. She felt like <i>she </i>should have been consulted first, and wants to make him stay. His mom actually has to come over and explain to this 'heroine' what a great job she did with her son, and butter her up to make her cool with it.<br><br><br><br>The constant tone of superiority and condescension hanging over this book like a cloud really put me off. At first, I wondered if I was maybe being too harsh on this book, so I kept reading, and the more I read, the less I liked. By the time I got to the end, I couldn't brush aside my qualms anymore. It had this galling "savior" tone to it, like the heroine was making it her personal mission to "humanize" the neurodivergent and it was her own personal discovery, and she expected <i>all the awards for it</i>. I went to look at the negative reviews for this book once I had finished and saw, to my relief, that I was not alone. Some people used the word "fetishization" and I think that's the word that was escaping me: Colton's hotness was basically used as an excuse to make him worth pursuing, in spite of what made him different, and the entire journey was one-sided and written entirely from a privileged, ableist perspective about <i>how brave </i>people are who bother befriending those who are different.<br><br><br><br>Thirdly, I really didn't like the slut-shaming and the way sexuality is treated in this book. It's a short book, and yet the 'heroine' is constantly making jabs at her friend, Harper. Oh, and this girl who gets chlamydia from a tanning bed is called "Chlam-face" - by the heroine, no less. Is the heroine innocent and pure? Of course. She's so innocent and pure that she's too afraid to get birth control from her parents, so she has a friend steal her some from a clinic. #InnocentAndPureFTW<br><br><br><br>For better romance novels about neurodiversity, I'd suggest K.J. Charles's AN UNSEEN ATTRACTION, and Jennifer Ashley's THE MADNESS OF LORD IAN MACKENZIE. Both are historical fiction, unfortunately, since I don't read too many contemporary romances, but I thought both did a fairly good job with this - although I will be honest that THE MADNESS (as the title might suggest) comes across as dated and shares many of the same issues as PUDDLE JUMPING.<br><br><br><br>This was a pretty terrible book. I took a nap before reviewing it so I wouldn't sound *too* cranky, but it still made me pretty irritated (as you can probably tell, haha). I wouldn't recommend it.<br><br><br><br>1 to 1.5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="6252552983088867999" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_933095757" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/933095757" />
    <a title="Stephanie Alexander" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4984664-stephanie-alexander"><img alt="Stephanie Alexander" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346077631p2/4984664.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/933095757?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephanie Alexander" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephanie Alexander" href="/user/show/4984664-stephanie-alexander">Stephanie Alexander</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/21825607-puddle-jumping">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4984664-stephanie-alexander?shelf=made-me-laugh-cry-sing-and-dance">made-me-laugh-cry-sing-and-dance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4984664-stephanie-alexander?shelf=couldnt-put-it-down">couldnt-put-it-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4984664-stephanie-alexander?shelf=amazing-amazing-amazing">amazing-amazing-amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4984664-stephanie-alexander?shelf=love-the-cover">love-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4984664-stephanie-alexander?shelf=july">july</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4984664-stephanie-alexander?shelf=fan-of-authors-previous-work">fan-of-authors-previous-work</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4984664-stephanie-alexander?shelf=love-the-author">love-the-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer933095757" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15432856817373615206">When ten year old Lilly is asked to babysit her neighbor Colton, all she sees is a sweet little boy who fascinates her. But after getting electrocuted (amongst other misadventures) and unintentionally putting Colton in danger, their friendship is abruptly severed...<br/><br/>Until years later, when Colton walks into her high school, and something in Lilly stirs.<br/><br/>Colton is still the extraordinary boy he was when they were little, only now he’s all grown up and Lilly really wants to know him better. After sh</span>
  <span id="freeText15432856817373615206" style="display:none">When ten year old Lilly is asked to babysit her neighbor Colton, all she sees is a sweet little boy who fascinates her. But after getting electrocuted (amongst other misadventures) and unintentionally putting Colton in danger, their friendship is abruptly severed...<br /><br />Until years later, when Colton walks into her high school, and something in Lilly stirs.<br /><br />Colton is still the extraordinary boy he was when they were little, only now he’s all grown up and Lilly really wants to know him better. After she spots him at a local fair selling his gorgeous paintings, Lilly knows that his talent far exceeds that of anyone she’s ever known. She realizes then, that he’s different, but it doesn't matter to her.<br /> <br />Lilly tries to learn everything she can about Asperger’s, because she knows that if she wants to be friends with him, then she needs to understand what makes him tick. Lilly does whatever it takes to help Colton, who has been sheltered for years, navigate in society amongst fellow highschoolers. And soon, she realizes that falling in love with Colton presents more challenges that any normal teenage relationship can guarantee. She also realizes that he’s worth it. Even when everything falls apart and she's left wondering what it means.<br /><br />This is the story of two friends reunited, who fall in love despite all the odds against them saying they shouldn’t. It’s honest, clearly well researched, touching, sometimes frustratingly heartbreaking, and beautifully written.<br /><br />My cousin belongs to an Autism support group for her teenage son, who has high functioning Autism. I gave an early version of this book to her when she was in a dark place- watching all the typical teenagers taking pictures outside before Prom and she was wondering if her son would ever find friendship, or even love. This is the story that gave her hope. <br /><br />After years of teaching children with high functioning Autism, and Asperger’s Syndrome, I have had students contact me later on in their teen years, regaling me with their accomplishments, their friendships with neurotypical peers, and their successful relationships. It's incredibly heartwarming to learn that everyone can be loved and love in return.<br /><br />One of the biggest problems with fictional literature that features Autistic characters is that they are often portrayed as disabled and incapable of love or relationships with non-Autistic partners. Amber Lynne Johnson has squashed that stereotype, giving her main character a voice of his own, and a realistic portrayal of what is possible between two people who care for one another despite what outside expectations dictate.<br /><br />I was enthralled with this book and so genuinely moved. And I am proud of her for facing such a controversial topic and doing it extraordinarily well.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15432856817373615206" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_899312176" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/899312176" />
    <a title="Kathie (katmom)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5153260-kathie-katmom"><img alt="Kathie (katmom)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1300650721p2/5153260.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/899312176?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathie (katmom)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathie (katmom)" href="/user/show/5153260-kathie-katmom">Kathie (katmom)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/21825607-puddle-jumping">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5153260-kathie-katmom?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer899312176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16839455363121467438"><b>OH MY GOSH!!! PUDDLE JUMPING is a nominee in the GOODREADS CHOICE AWARDS!!!! If you read it and loved it, please consider VOTING FOR it! <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/choiceawards/best-young-adult-fiction-books-2014'>https://www.goodreads.com/choiceaward...</a> </b><br/><br/>I was blessed to be an editor for Puddle Jumping. Have to confess that I had to keep going back and rereading because I'd forget that I was EDITING...and would just READ. That's the sign of a good book, at least in my opinion!<br/><br/>Colton is an artist. He's one of those genius artists that start young, and improve even more ov</span>
  <span id="freeText16839455363121467438" style="display:none"><b>OH MY GOSH!!! PUDDLE JUMPING is a nominee in the GOODREADS CHOICE AWARDS!!!! If you read it and loved it, please consider VOTING FOR it! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/choiceawards/best-young-adult-fiction-books-2014">https://www.goodreads.com/choiceaward...</a> </b><br /><br />I was blessed to be an editor for Puddle Jumping. Have to confess that I had to keep going back and rereading because I'd forget that I was EDITING...and would just READ. That's the sign of a good book, at least in my opinion!<br /><br />Colton is an artist. He's one of those genius artists that start young, and improve even more over time. When he talks about art, adults listen. When people of all ages look at his work, they are enthralled. Lilly remembers when she tried to teach him to color in the lines. She didn't understand then, but she's starting to understand now. <br /><br />When Colton enrolls in her school for their senior year, Lilly figures it's time to learn who he really is beyond the artist savant that others admire.<br /><br />One of the many things that impressed me with Puddle Jumping, was the amount of research that went into the writing of it. Ms. Johnson kept this real. At one point, Colton and Lilly are watching some Hollywood flick about a guy with Asperger's. She doesn't want their relationship defined by what others think. She and Colton both want to experience life in a "normal" way. Of course, as my husband says, normal is a range, not a point. <br /><br />Puddle Jumping is a romance. It's a story of two young people coming of age and finding their way, together. It will make you smile, maybe cry a tear or two, and in the end? Well, it will be a couple hours well spent. I hope you enjoy it as much as I did, and maybe, you'll come away knowing a bit more about people who are in the <i>range</i> of normal. <br /><br />Puddle Jumping comes out on July 1, 2014...and I can't wait to hold a copy in my hands!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16839455363121467438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5238864683492408708"><b>5 ‘Emotional Watercolory Journey’ Stars </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414748317i/11686230.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i> Life is meant to be lived, and if you’re offered the chance to experience exceptional things with an extraordinary person, then there isn’t one reason in the world to say no. </i>
</b><br/><br/>My God it’s after such a long time that I’ve cried over a book this much. This is my first book by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7336499.Amber_L__Johnson' title='Amber L. Johnson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amber L. Johnson</a> and I’m definitely going to check more of her works. The story is narrated by Lily and I love her way of thinking, she is funny, silly and interact with the readers</span>
  <span id="freeText5238864683492408708" style="display:none"><b>5 ‘Emotional Watercolory Journey’ Stars </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414748317i/11686230.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i> Life is meant to be lived, and if you’re offered the chance to experience exceptional things with an extraordinary person, then there isn’t one reason in the world to say no. </i>
</b><br><br>My God it’s after such a long time that I’ve cried over a book this much. This is my first book by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7336499.Amber_L__Johnson" title="Amber L. Johnson" rel="nofollow noopener">Amber L. Johnson</a> and I’m definitely going to check more of her works. The story is narrated by Lily and I love her way of thinking, she is funny, silly and interact with the readers in her mind. Her Inner monologues are hilarious. I absolutely loved Colton, I mean who didn't fell in love with that guy if you’ve read the book of course and if you haven’t then I’ll say you are missing one of the most wonderful love stories ever written. <br><br>Little glimpse at Lily’s reaction when she met Colton<br><b>
  <i> God. Do you have any idea what was going on inside my body? It was like Christmas lights dropped in a puddle of water. I felt electrocuted by his gaze. Those eyes, still so trusting, still so observant, raked over my face just to stare silently. </i>

<div id="review_964482218" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/964482218" />
    <a title="Sydney Logan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6508080-sydney-logan"><img alt="Sydney Logan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475878207p2/6508080.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/964482218?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sydney Logan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sydney Logan" href="/user/show/6508080-sydney-logan">Sydney Logan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/21825607-puddle-jumping">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6508080-sydney-logan?shelf=new-adult-favorites">new-adult-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6508080-sydney-logan?shelf=novella">novella</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6508080-sydney-logan?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer964482218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8747176653895614203">I was so excited to receive an ARC copy of Puddle Jumping. While I love to read, it's been a long time since I've sat down and read a book, even a novella, all in one day. I couldn't put this down until I'd read every last word.<br/><br/>Puddle Jumping, at its heart, is the story of a boy and a girl. Simple, right? But love is never simple, and it can be even more complicated when Autism and Asperger's come into play. Love is supposed to be patient and kind, and that was definitely the case with Lilly and</span>
  <span id="freeText8747176653895614203" style="display:none">I was so excited to receive an ARC copy of Puddle Jumping. While I love to read, it's been a long time since I've sat down and read a book, even a novella, all in one day. I couldn't put this down until I'd read every last word.<br /><br />Puddle Jumping, at its heart, is the story of a boy and a girl. Simple, right? But love is never simple, and it can be even more complicated when Autism and Asperger's come into play. Love is supposed to be patient and kind, and that was definitely the case with Lilly and Colton. When you love someone who struggles with socialization and communication, that patience can be put to the test, no matter how much you love them.<br /><br />In Puddle Jumping, the author offers a beautiful, sensitive, and realistic portrayal of a young man struggling to just <i>be</i>. To be a son, a friend, a boyfriend, and a man. Amber Johnson has no idea how wonderful her writing really is. I plan to keep telling her until she believes it.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8747176653895614203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books" href="/user/show/6245313-kat-kitty-kats-crazy-about-books">❥ KAT ❥ Kitty Kats Crazy About Books</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1670992668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15920165079088291196"><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=kdwp50' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466162437i/19447085._SY540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>TITLE:</b> Puddle Jumping<br/><b>SERIES:</b> (Puddle Jumping, #1) <br/><b>AUTHOR:</b> Amber L. Johnson<br/><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance<br/><b>CHAPTERS:</b> 17<br/><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> June 29th 2014 <br/><br/><b>MY RATING</b><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=67tcac' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466162437i/19447086.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2wfmxab' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466163571i/19447371._SX540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This was recommended to me because I'd hit a book funk at the time, an oldie that's been sitting on my ipad for a while now and I am keen to see what journey this author is going to take me on with this book. <br/><br/><b> PUDDLE JUMPING: </b> Puddle Jumping is told from Lilly's perspective and is kind of told in diary format. This is the story about L</span>
  <span id="freeText15920165079088291196" style="display:none"><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=kdwp50" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466162437i/19447085._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>TITLE:</b> Puddle Jumping<br><b>SERIES:</b> (Puddle Jumping, #1) <br><b>AUTHOR:</b> Amber L. Johnson<br><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>CHAPTERS:</b> 17<br><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> June 29th 2014 <br><br><b>MY RATING</b><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=67tcac" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466162437i/19447086.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2wfmxab" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466163571i/19447371._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was recommended to me because I'd hit a book funk at the time, an oldie that's been sitting on my ipad for a while now and I am keen to see what journey this author is going to take me on with this book. <br><br><b> PUDDLE JUMPING: </b> Puddle Jumping is told from Lilly's perspective and is kind of told in diary format. This is the story about Lily &amp; Colton, these two meet when Colton is 9 and Lilly is 10, she's his babysitter and finds it strange that she's getting paid to babysit a boy whose not that much younger than her.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=hwmxlf" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466140174i/19443895.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>This isn't you run of the mill fairy tale. It is not some Harlequin romance. I wouldn't even categorize this as much of a romance at all. Because I'm not the kind of person to fall in love. And neither is the guy I'm head over heals for.</i><br><br><i>
  <b> I don't believe there's such a thing as conventional love<br>Love is bending<br>Love is breaking<br>Love is constantly learning.</b>
</i><br><br>Colton is a quiet, withdrawn, young boy who lives in his own world whose passion is drawing and painting. Lily is what you would call an accident prone young girl who is always getting herself into scrapes and needs rescuing twice from Colton himself.<br><br><i>
  <b> When we were kids<br>I almost died every-time we were together<br>I'm a mess<br>I'm chaos </b>
</i><br><br>Lily always knew there was something different about Colton but isn't told until she's 15 when they meet again that he has Aspergers.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=hwmxlf" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466140174i/19443895.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>I loved a boy who was extraordinary beyond words.</i><br><br><i>
  <b> It took me five years to figure out exactly what was so different<br>about Colton Neely.</b>
</i><br><br>This is what I'd class as a second chance romance, it's not until their college years that their friendship/relationship grows into so much more.<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=hwmxlf" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466140174i/19443895.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><i>Your're my quiet, Lilly<br>For as long as I can remember <br>You've been the one to calm me down.</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2wfmxab" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466163571i/19447371._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A few times I felt my eyes prickling with tears, then the next moment I'd be giggling, sighing over my love for these two, this was just amazingly well written, there's nothing I would change about this book. No words really describe the feels that raced through me when reading this..<br><br>I am so glad I took that leap and one clicked this after the recommendation to read it. <br><br>Such a unique, beautifully thought provoking read that has claimed a piece of my heart forever. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('amZS/j27myXsEf9mza4nuN0oyy3FkYFXAYrW3Ol1ZUfYznGlZGe4wZua7uMC4Ao5K+re6ySrdAxST6FToBbeKg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('iDwljzg5XtQDsBP8KJ8Sejy3ZEViCydBheGFJbFMtpI6lAbUYeV9MHQ7Annn0T/7ynVxg4Mx0hrWJPKq+C8N/w==')})
  }
